2025-08-03T08:08:13Z This GitHub issue describes a CI/CD workflow for building, packaging, and releasing the "StreamGod" Windows software. The workflow is triggered on pushes to the main branch or can be manually initiated. It installs dependencies, builds the Electron app, sets up NSIS for creating an installer, and optionally signs the binaries using a provided signing certificate. The workflow handles bundling outputs into a portable EXE, an NSIS installer, and a flashdrive-ready ZIP bundle containing all required components, including documentation and fallback assets. Finally, it creates a GitHub release with versioned tagging, attaches the compiled assets (installer and ZIP bundle) to the release, and publishes it. Secrets are used for signing and GitHub token authentication.
